control (`ssoSettingsApi` feature flag) implements a comprehensive, multi-layered architecture that gates the entire Single Sign-On settings infrastructure. This control extends from feature flag definition through to API endpoints, OAuth connector wiring, and access control enforcement.\\n\\n### Layer 1: Feature Flag Definition\\n\\nThe `ssoSettingsApi` feature flag is centrally defined in **pkg/services/featuremgmt/registry.go** (lines 933-941) with metadata:\\n- **Name**: \\\"ssoSettingsApi\\\"\\n- **Description**: \\\"Enables the SSO settings API and the OAuth configuration UIs in Grafana\\\"\\n- **Stage**: FeatureStageGeneralAvailability (GA)\\n- **Expression**: \\\"true\\\" (enabled by default)\\n- **AllowSelfServe**: true (users can **pkg/services/featuremgmt/toggles_gen.json**: JSON representation for API exposure\\n\\n### Layer 2: SSO Settings Infrastructure\\n\\nThe SSO settings infrastructure establishes two core interfaces in **pkg/services/ssosettings/ssosettings.go**:\\n\\n**Service Interface** (lines 15-37):\\n- `List()`, `ListWithRedactedSecrets()`: Retrieve all SSO settings\\n- `GetForProvider()`, `GetForProviderWithRedactedSecrets()`: Retrieve settings for specific provider\\n- `Upsert()`: Create or update SSO settings with audit trail\\n- `Delete()`: Soft-delete SSO settings\\n- `Patch()`: Update key-value pairs in SSO settings\\n- `RegisterReloadable(provider string, reloadable Reloadable)`: Register a provider for live configuration reloading\\n- `Reload(ctx context.Context, provider
